OBJECT Report 14000707 Package SED
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=06/28/17;
    Time=12:00:00 PM;
    Version List=SE0.52.19;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Package SED;
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   CLEAR(ReportAction);
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  CompanyInfo.GET;
                  GetPackingStation;
                  ShippingSetup.GET;

                  IF PackingStation."Federal ID No." <> '' THEN
                    TaxID := PackingStation."Federal ID No."
                  ELSE BEGIN
                    CompanyInfo.TESTFIELD("VAT Registration No.");
                    TaxID := CompanyInfo."VAT Registration No.";
                  END;

                  CLEAR(FromAddress);
                  FromAddress[1] := PackingStation."Ship-from Company";
                  FromAddress[2] := PackingStation."Ship-from Address";
                  IF PackingStation."Ship-from Address2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                    FromAddress[3] := PackingStation."Ship-from Address2";
                    FromAddress[4] :=
                      PackingStation."Ship-from City" + ', ' + PackingStation."Ship-from State" + ', US';
                  END ELSE
                    FromAddress[3] :=
                      PackingStation."Ship-from City" + ', ' + PackingStation."Ship-from State" + ', US';
                  FromZipCode := PackingStation."Ship-from ZIP Code";
                  FromState := PackingStation."Ship-from State";
                  IF PackingStation."Export License Exception" <> '' THEN
                    ExportLicense := PackingStation."Export License Exception"
                  ELSE
                    ExportLicense := PackingStation."Export License No.";
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 6656;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table14000701;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Source Type,Source Subtype,Source ID)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               Package2@1240030000 : Record 14000701;
                               PackageLine@1240030001 : Record 14000702;
                             BEGIN
                               IF (ReportAction <> ReportAction::"Print Blank Form") AND
                                  ((GETFILTER("Source Type") = '') OR
                                   (GETFILTER("Source ID") = '')) AND
                                  (GETFILTER("No.") = '')
                                 THEN
                                   ERROR(Text001);

                               IF ((GETFILTER("Source Type") <> '') OR
                                   (GETFILTER("Source ID") <> '')) AND
                                  (GETFILTER("No.") <> '')
                                 THEN
                                   ERROR(Text002,FIELDCAPTION("Source ID"),FIELDCAPTION("No."));

                               CLEAR(FinalConsignee);
                               ShipmentDate := WORKDATE;

                               IF GETFILTER("Source ID") <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                 Package2.SETCURRENTKEY("Source Type","Source Subtype","Source ID");
                                 Package2.COPYFILTERS(Package);
                                 IF Package2.FIND('-') AND
                                    Package2."Multi Document Package"
                                 THEN
                                    SETFILTER("Source ID",Package2."Multi Document No.");

                                 Package2.RESET;
                                 Package2.SETCURRENTKEY("Source Type","Source Subtype","Source ID");
                               END;

                               IF (GETFILTER("Source ID") <> '') OR
                                  (GETFILTER("No.") <> '')
                               THEN BEGIN
                                 Package2.COPYFILTERS(Package);
                                 IF Package2.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                                   PackageFound := TRUE;
                                   FinalConsignee[1] := Package2."Ship-to Name";
                                   FinalConsignee[2] := Package2."Ship-to Address";
                                   IF Package2."Ship-to Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                     FinalConsignee[3] := Package2."Ship-to Address 2";
                                     IF Package2."Ship-to State" <> '' THEN
                                       FinalConsignee[4] :=
                                         Package2."Ship-to City" + ', ' + Package2."Ship-to State" + '  ' + Package2."Ship-to ZIP Code"
                                     ELSE
                                       FinalConsignee[4] := Package2."Ship-to City" + '  ' + Package2."Ship-to ZIP Code";
                                     FinalConsignee[5] := Package2."Ship-to Country Code";
                                   END ELSE BEGIN
                                     IF Package2."Ship-to State" <> '' THEN
                                       FinalConsignee[3] :=
                                         Package2."Ship-to City" + ', ' + Package2."Ship-to State" + '  ' + Package2."Ship-to ZIP Code"
                                     ELSE
                                     FinalConsignee[3] := Package2."Ship-to City" + '  ' + Package2."Ship-to ZIP Code";
                                     FinalConsignee[4] := Package2."Ship-to Country Code";
                                   END;
                                   ShipmentDate := WORKDATE;

                                   ShippingAgent.GET(Package2."Shipping Agent Code");
                                   EShipAgentService.GET(
                                     Package2."Shipping Agent Code",
                                     Package2."Shipping Agent Service",
                                     Package2."World Wide Service");
                                   IF EShipAgentService."Transport Method Type" = EShipAgentService."Transport Method Type"::Air
                                   THEN BEGIN
                                     TransportationMethod := 'AIR';
                                     PortOfExport := PackingStation."Ship-from Airport Code";
                                   END ELSE
                                     TransportationMethod := 'GROUND';

                                   CASE ShippingAgent."Shipper Type" OF
                                     ShippingAgent."Shipper Type"::UPS:
                                       BEGIN
                                         CarrierName := 'UPS';
                                         GetUPSPackageInfo(Package2."No.");
                                       END;
                                     ShippingAgent."Shipper Type"::FEDEX:
                                       BEGIN
                                         CarrierName := 'Federal Express';
                                         GetFedExPackageInfo(Package2."No.");
                                       END;
                                   END;

                                   REPEAT
                                     PackageLine.RESET;
                                     PackageLine.SETRANGE("Package No.",Package2."No.");
                                     PackageLine.SETFILTER("Export Controls Class No.",'<>%1','');
                                     IF PackageLine.FIND('+') THEN
                                       ECCN := PackageLine."Export Controls Class No.";
                                     IF (NOT LineFound) AND
                                        (ReportAction <> ReportAction::"Print Blank Form")
                                     THEN BEGIN
                                       PackageLine.SETRANGE("Export Controls Class No.");
                                       IF PackageLine.FIND('+') THEN
                                         LineFound := TRUE;
                                     END;
                                   UNTIL (Package2.NEXT = 0) OR LineFound;
                                 END;
                               END;
                             END;

               ReqFilterFields=Source Type,Source ID }

               DataItemTable=Table14000702;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Package No.,Line No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Type=CONST(Item),

                                  TempPackageLine.INSERT;
                                END;

    { 8762;    ;DataItem;SummarizeItems      ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempPackageLine.SETCURRENTKEY(Type,"No.");
                               IF TempPackageLine.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
                                 REPEAT
                                   NumberOfLines := NumberOfLines + 1;
                                 UNTIL TempPackageLine.NEXT = 0;
                                 TempPackageLine.FIND('-');
                                 TempPrevPackageLine := TempPackageLine;
                               END;
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,NumberOfLines);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF TempPackageLine."No." <> TempPrevPackageLine."No." THEN BEGIN
                                    TempItemSummary := TempPrevPackageLine;
                                    TempItemSummary."Value (Price)" := TotalPrice;
                                    TempItemSummary."Gross Weight" := GetWeightKG(TotalWeight);
                                    TempItemSummary.INSERT;
                                    TempPrevPackageLine := TempPackageLine;
                                    TotalPrice := TempPackageLine."Value (Price)";
                                    TotalWeight := TempPackageLine.GetWeight;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    TotalPrice := TotalPrice + TempPackageLine."Value (Price)";
                                    TotalWeight := TotalWeight + TempPackageLine.GetWeight;
                                  END;

                                  IF TempPackageLine.NEXT = 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    TempItemSummary := TempPrevPackageLine;
                                    TempItemSummary."Value (Price)" := TotalPrice;
                                    TempItemSummary."Gross Weight" := GetWeightKG(TotalWeight);
                                    TempItemSummary.INSERT;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 3955;    ;DataItem;PrintSummaryItemLines;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempItemSummary.SETCURRENTKEY(Type,"No.");
                               NumberOfLines := 0;

                               IF TempItemSummary.FIND('-') THEN
                                 REPEAT
                                   NumberOfLines := NumberOfLines + 1;
                                 UNTIL TempItemSummary.NEXT = 0;

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,NumberOfLines);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF OnLine = 0 THEN
                                    TempItemSummary.FIND('-')
                                  ELSE
                                    TempItemSummary.NEXT;
                                  OnLine := OnLine + 1;

                                  IF (TempItemSummary."Country of Manufacture" <> '') AND
                                     (TempItemSummary."Country of Manufacture" <> 'US')
                                  THEN
                                    ItemExportCode := 'F'
                                  ELSE
                                    ItemExportCode := 'D';
                                END;
                                 }

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPackingStation@51();
    BEGIN
      IF PackingStation.Code = '' THEN
        PackingStation.GetPackingStation;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetUPSPackageInfo@2(PackageNo@1240030000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      UPSOptionPage@1240030001 : Record 14000761;
    BEGIN
      UPSOptionPage.GET(UPSOptionPage.Type::Package,PackageNo);
      WaybillNo := DELCHR(UPSOptionPage."Waybill No.");
      RelatedX := '';
      NotRelatedX := '';
      IF UPSOptionPage."Consignee Related to Shipper" THEN
        RelatedX := 'X'
      ELSE
        NotRelatedX := 'X';
      HazardX := '';
      NotHazardX := '';

      IF (UPSOptionPage."Dangerous Goods") OR (UPSOptionPage."Dry Ice") THEN
        HazardX := 'X'
      ELSE
        NotHazardX := 'X';

      IF UPSOptionPage."Importer Name" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(Importer);
        Importer[1] := UPSOptionPage."Importer Name";
        Importer[2] := UPSOptionPage."Importer Address";

        IF UPSOptionPage."Impoter Address 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          Importer[3] := UPSOptionPage."Impoter Address 2";

          IF UPSOptionPage."Importer State" <> '' THEN
            Importer[4] :=
              UPSOptionPage."Importer City" + ', ' +
              UPSOptionPage."Importer State" + '  ' +
              UPSOptionPage."Importer ZIP Code"
          ELSE
            Importer[4] :=
              UPSOptionPage."Importer City" + '  ' + UPSOptionPage."Importer ZIP Code";

          Importer[5] := UPSOptionPage."Importer Country Code";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          IF UPSOptionPage."Importer State" <> '' THEN
            Importer[3] :=
              UPSOptionPage."Importer City" + ', ' +
              UPSOptionPage."Importer State" + '  ' +
              UPSOptionPage."Importer ZIP Code"
          ELSE
            Importer[3] :=
              UPSOptionPage."Importer City" + '  ' + UPSOptionPage."Importer ZIP Code";

          Importer[4] := UPSOptionPage."Importer Country Code";
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetFedExPackageInfo@4(PackageNo@1240030000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      FedExOptionPage@1240030001 : Record 14000781;
    BEGIN
      FedExOptionPage.GET(FedExOptionPage.Type::Package,PackageNo);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetWeightKG@1240030003(Weight@1240030000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF ShippingSetup."Default Weight Units" = ShippingSetup."Default Weight Units"::LBS THEN
        EXIT(ROUND(ShippingSetup.PoundToKilo(Weight),0.001))
      ELSE
        EXIT(ROUND(Weight,0.001));
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
